1. Project Overview
1.1 What You Are Building
A full-stack web application where users enter their zodiac sign, birth month, and a personal preference to receive a list of recommended gemstones. An admin can manage the gemstone catalog. The app demonstrates CRUD operations, JWT authentication, REST API design, and React with Tailwind CSS — exactly what campus placement evaluators look for.

1.2 Scope Constraints (48-Hour Rules)

1.3 What This Project Demonstrates
Full-stack architecture: React SPA + Node/Express REST API + MongoDB
Authentication with JWT and role-based routing (user vs admin)
Complete CRUD operations: gemstone catalog management by admin
Search and filter functionality on a live data catalog
Recommendation logic: rule-based engine using a JSON configuration
Persistent recommendation history per user
Responsive Tailwind CSS UI across mobile and desktop
Clean folder structure and code organization
2. System Architecture
2.1 Overview
A straightforward three-layer architecture: React SPA served from Vercel, Node/Express API on Render, MongoDB Atlas as the database. No load balancer, no Redis, no microservices — a single deployable backend process.

2.2 High-Level Architecture Diagram (Mermaid)
📊  Paste the Mermaid code block below into mermaid.live to render the diagram.

graph TD
    subgraph Frontend["Frontend — Vercel (Free)"]
        React["React SPA\nTailwind CSS\nReact Router v6"]
    end

    subgraph Backend["Backend — Render (Free)"]
        Express["Node.js + Express.js\nREST API\n:10000"]
    end

    subgraph Database["Database — MongoDB Atlas (Free M0)"]
        Mongo["MongoDB\nusers | gemstones | recommendations"]
    end

    React <-->|"HTTPS REST API\n(Axios + JWT Bearer)"| Express
    Express <-->|"Mongoose ODM"| Mongo

    style Frontend fill:#ECFDF5,stroke:#059669
    style Backend fill:#EFF6FF,stroke:#3B82F6
    style Database fill:#FEF3C7,stroke:#D97706


2.3 Request Flow

Browser Request
  → React Component (onClick / form submit)
  → Axios API call  (attaches JWT: Authorization: Bearer <token>)
  → Express Router  (matches route)
  → Auth Middleware  (verifies JWT, attaches req.user)
  → Controller       (calls service / model)
  → Mongoose Model   (query MongoDB)
  → JSON Response    (success / error)
  → React State Update → UI Re-render


💡  48-hour tip: Build and test one route at a time. Start with /auth/register, confirm it works in Postman, then move to the next endpoint. Never wire frontend before the backend route is confirmed working.

3.2 ER Diagram (Mermaid)
📊  Paste the Mermaid code block below into mermaid.live to render the diagram.

erDiagram
    USERS {
        ObjectId _id PK
        string name
        string email UK
        string password
        string role
        string zodiacSign
        int birthMonth
        string preference
        date createdAt
    }

    GEMSTONES {
        ObjectId _id PK
        string name UK
        string description
        string[] zodiacSigns
        string[] birthMonths
        string category
        string color
        string imageUrl
        number price
        boolean inStock
        date createdAt
    }

    RECOMMENDATIONS {
        ObjectId _id PK
        ObjectId userId FK
        string zodiacSign
        int birthMonth
        string preference
        ObjectId[] gemstoneIds FK
        date createdAt
    }

    USERS ||--o{ RECOMMENDATIONS : "requests"
    GEMSTONES }o--o{ RECOMMENDATIONS : "appears in"


3.3 MongoDB Schemas (Mongoose)
User Schema  —  models/User.js

const mongoose = require('mongoose');
const bcrypt   = require('bcryptjs');

const userSchema = new mongoose.Schema({
  name:       { type: String, required: true, trim: true },
  email:      { type: String, required: true, unique: true, lowercase: true },
  password:   { type: String, required: true, select: false },
  role:       { type: String, enum: ['user','admin'], default: 'user' },
  zodiacSign: { type: String, enum: ['Aries','Taurus','Gemini','Cancer','Leo',
               'Virgo','Libra','Scorpio','Sagittarius','Capricorn','Aquarius','Pisces'] },
  birthMonth: { type: Number, min: 1, max: 12 },
  preference: { type: String, enum: ['healing','protection','wealth',
               'love','clarity','energy'], default: 'healing' }
}, { timestamps: true });

userSchema.pre('save', async function(next) {
  if (!this.isModified('password')) return next();
  this.password = await bcrypt.hash(this.password, 10);
  next();
});

userSchema.methods.matchPassword = function(entered) {
  return require('bcryptjs').compare(entered, this.password);
};

module.exports = mongoose.model('User', userSchema);


Gemstone Schema  —  models/Gemstone.js

const mongoose = require('mongoose');

const gemstoneSchema = new mongoose.Schema({
  name:        { type: String, required: true, unique: true, trim: true },
  description: { type: String, required: true },
  zodiacSigns: [{ type: String }],          // e.g. ['Aries','Leo']
  birthMonths: [{ type: Number }],          // e.g. [1, 8]  (Jan, Aug)
  category:    { type: String,              // 'healing' | 'protection' etc.
                 enum: ['healing','protection','wealth','love','clarity','energy'] },
  color:       { type: String, required: true },
  imageUrl:    { type: String, default: '' },
  price:       { type: Number, default: 0 },
  inStock:     { type: Boolean, default: true }
}, { timestamps: true });

gemstoneSchema.index({ name: 1 });
gemstoneSchema.index({ zodiacSigns: 1, birthMonths: 1, category: 1 });

module.exports = mongoose.model('Gemstone', gemstoneSchema);


Recommendation Schema  —  models/Recommendation.js

const mongoose = require('mongoose');

const recommendationSchema = new mongoose.Schema({
  userId:      { type: mongoose.Schema.Types.ObjectId, ref: 'User', required: true },
  zodiacSign:  { type: String, required: true },
  birthMonth:  { type: Number, required: true },
  preference:  { type: String, required: true },
  gemstones:   [{ type: mongoose.Schema.Types.ObjectId, ref: 'Gemstone' }]
}, { timestamps: true });

recommendationSchema.index({ userId: 1, createdAt: -1 });

module.exports = mongoose.model('Recommendation', recommendationSchema);

4.3 Request & Response Examples
POST /auth/register
Request body:

{
  "name": "Ashish Khatri",
  "email": "ashish@example.com",
  "password": "Pass@1234",
  "zodiacSign": "Scorpio",
  "birthMonth": 11,
  "preference": "healing"
}

Response 201:

{
  "success": true,
  "token": "eyJhbGciOiJIUzI1NiIsInR5cCI6IkpXVCJ9...",
  "user": {
    "_id": "64fa...",
    "name": "Ashish Khatri",
    "email": "ashish@example.com",
    "role": "user",
    "zodiacSign": "Scorpio",
    "birthMonth": 11,
    "preference": "healing"
  }
}


POST /recommendations/generate
Request body (user's profile data is sent from frontend):

{
  "zodiacSign": "Scorpio",
  "birthMonth": 11,
  "preference": "healing"
}

Response 200:

{
  "success": true,
  "recommendationId": "64fc...",
  "gemstones": [
    {
      "_id": "64fb...",
      "name": "Amethyst",
      "description": "A violet quartz promoting calm and clarity.",
      "color": "Violet",
      "category": "healing",
      "imageUrl": "https://example.com/amethyst.jpg",
      "price": 850
    },
    { "name": "Black Tourmaline", ... },
    { "name": "Obsidian", ... }
  ]
}


GET /admin/stats
Response 200:

{
  "success": true,
  "stats": {
    "totalUsers": 42,
    "totalGemstones": 20,
    "totalRecommendations": 138,
    "mostPopularZodiac": "Scorpio"
  }
}


4.4 Standardized Error Response

// All errors follow this shape:
{
  "success": false,
  "message": "Human-readable error message"
}

// HTTP status codes used:
// 200  OK
// 201  Created
// 400  Bad Request (validation failure)
// 401  Unauthorized (no/invalid JWT)
// 403  Forbidden (role mismatch)
// 404  Not Found
// 500  Server Error


4.5 JWT Middleware

// middleware/auth.js
const jwt  = require('jsonwebtoken');
const User = require('../models/User');

exports.protect = async (req, res, next) => {
  const header = req.headers.authorization;
  if (!header || !header.startsWith('Bearer ')) {
    return res.status(401).json({ success: false, message: 'Not authenticated' });
  }
  const token = header.split(' ')[1];
  try {
    const decoded = jwt.verify(token, process.env.JWT_SECRET);
    req.user = await User.findById(decoded.id);
    next();
  } catch {
    return res.status(401).json({ success: false, message: 'Invalid token' });
  }
};

exports.adminOnly = (req, res, next) => {
  if (req.user?.role !== 'admin') {
    return res.status(403).json({ success: false, message: 'Admin only' });
  }
  next();
};

5. Folder Structure
5.1 Backend  /server

server/
├── config/
│   └── db.js                  ← MongoDB connection
│
├── controllers/
│   ├── authController.js      ← register, login
│   ├── userController.js      ← getMe, updateMe
│   ├── gemstoneController.js  ← CRUD + search
│   ├── recommendationController.js
│   └── adminController.js     ← stats, user list
│
├── middleware/
│   ├── auth.js                ← protect, adminOnly
│   └── errorHandler.js        ← global error middleware
│
├── models/
│   ├── User.js
│   ├── Gemstone.js
│   └── Recommendation.js
│
├── routes/
│   ├── authRoutes.js
│   ├── userRoutes.js
│   ├── gemstoneRoutes.js
│   ├── recommendationRoutes.js
│   └── adminRoutes.js
│
├── data/
│   ├── recommendationMap.js   ← JSON engine (see Section 6)
│   └── seedGemstones.js       ← 20 gemstone seed records
│
├── .env
├── package.json
└── server.js                  ← Express entry point


5.2 Frontend  /client

client/
├── public/
│   └── index.html
│
└── src/
    ├── api/
    │   └── axios.js           ← Axios instance with JWT interceptor
    │
    ├── components/
    │   ├── Navbar.jsx
    │   ├── GemstoneCard.jsx
    │   ├── ProtectedRoute.jsx ← redirects if not logged in
    │   ├── AdminRoute.jsx     ← redirects if not admin
    │   └── Loader.jsx
    │
    ├── context/
    │   └── AuthContext.jsx    ← global user + token state
    │
    ├── pages/
    │   ├── Home.jsx           ← landing / search
    │   ├── Login.jsx
    │   ├── Register.jsx
    │   ├── Profile.jsx        ← view + edit profile
    │   ├── Catalog.jsx        ← browse + search gemstones
    │   ├── Recommend.jsx      ← run + view recommendations
    │   ├── History.jsx        ← recommendation history
    │   └── admin/
    │       └── Dashboard.jsx  ← stats + gemstone CRUD + user list
    │
    ├── App.jsx                ← React Router setup
    └── main.jsx               ← ReactDOM entry


5.3 server.js  —  Express Entry Point

const express    = require('express');
const cors       = require('cors');
const connectDB  = require('./config/db');
require('dotenv').config();

connectDB();

const app = express();
app.use(cors({ origin: process.env.CLIENT_URL }));
app.use(express.json());

app.use('/api/auth',            require('./routes/authRoutes'));
app.use('/api/users',           require('./routes/userRoutes'));
app.use('/api/gemstones',       require('./routes/gemstoneRoutes'));
app.use('/api/recommendations', require('./routes/recommendationRoutes'));
app.use('/api/admin',           require('./routes/adminRoutes'));

app.use(require('./middleware/errorHandler'));

const PORT = process.env.PORT || 5000;
app.listen(PORT, () => console.log(`Server running on port ${PORT}`));

6.2 React Router Setup  —  App.jsx

import { BrowserRouter, Routes, Route } from 'react-router-dom';
import Navbar          from './components/Navbar';
import ProtectedRoute  from './components/ProtectedRoute';
import AdminRoute      from './components/AdminRoute';
import Home            from './pages/Home';
import Login           from './pages/Login';
import Register        from './pages/Register';
import Catalog         from './pages/Catalog';
import Recommend       from './pages/Recommend';
import History         from './pages/History';
import Profile         from './pages/Profile';
import Dashboard       from './pages/admin/Dashboard';

export default function App() {
  return (
    <BrowserRouter>
      <Navbar />
      <Routes>
        <Route path="/"          element={<Home />} />
        <Route path="/login"     element={<Login />} />
        <Route path="/register"  element={<Register />} />
        <Route path="/catalog"   element={<Catalog />} />
        <Route path="/recommend" element={<ProtectedRoute><Recommend /></ProtectedRoute>} />
        <Route path="/history"   element={<ProtectedRoute><History /></ProtectedRoute>} />
        <Route path="/profile"   element={<ProtectedRoute><Profile /></ProtectedRoute>} />
        <Route path="/admin"     element={<AdminRoute><Dashboard /></AdminRoute>} />
      </Routes>
    </BrowserRouter>
  );
}


6.3 Auth Context  —  context/AuthContext.jsx

import { createContext, useContext, useState, useEffect } from 'react';

const AuthContext = createContext(null);

export function AuthProvider({ children }) {
  const [user,  setUser]  = useState(null);
  const [token, setToken] = useState(localStorage.getItem('token'));

  // On mount: load user from localStorage if token exists
  useEffect(() => {
    const saved = localStorage.getItem('user');
    if (saved) setUser(JSON.parse(saved));
  }, []);

  const login = (userData, jwt) => {
    setUser(userData);
    setToken(jwt);
    localStorage.setItem('user',  JSON.stringify(userData));
    localStorage.setItem('token', jwt);
  };

  const logout = () => {
    setUser(null);
    setToken(null);
    localStorage.removeItem('user');
    localStorage.removeItem('token');
  };

  return (
    <AuthContext.Provider value={{ user, token, login, logout }}>
      {children}
    </AuthContext.Provider>
  );
}

export const useAuth = () => useContext(AuthContext);

⚠️  Token stored in localStorage is simple and works for placement demos. In production, use HttpOnly cookies. Be prepared to explain this trade-off if asked.

6.4 Axios Instance  —  api/axios.js

import axios from 'axios';

const API = axios.create({ baseURL: import.meta.env.VITE_API_URL || 'http://localhost:5000/api' });

// Attach JWT to every request automatically
API.interceptors.request.use(config => {
  const token = localStorage.getItem('token');
  if (token) config.headers.Authorization = `Bearer ${token}`;
  return config;
});

export default API;

7. Recommendation Engine
7.1 Design Philosophy
The engine is a pure JSON lookup — no AI, no weighted scoring, no external API. It is fast, transparent, and completely interview-explainable. The logic fits in two files and under 60 lines of code.

7.2 How It Works
Step 1 — Start with the zodiac map to get gemstone names for the user's zodiac sign
Step 2 — Query MongoDB for Gemstones where name is in that list AND birthMonths includes the user's birth month (if any match, prioritize them)
Step 3 — From that result, further filter by category matching the user's preference
Step 4 — If fewer than 3 results, fall back to zodiac-only matches
Step 5 — Return up to 5 gemstones, save as a Recommendation document

7.3 Zodiac Map JSON  —  data/recommendationMap.js

const ZODIAC_GEMS = {
  Aries:       ['Ruby', 'Red Coral', 'Carnelian', 'Bloodstone'],
  Taurus:      ['Emerald', 'Rose Quartz', 'Sapphire', 'Malachite'],
  Gemini:      ['Citrine', 'Agate', 'Tiger Eye', 'Aquamarine'],
  Cancer:      ['Moonstone', 'Pearl', 'Labradorite', 'Ruby'],
  Leo:         ['Peridot', 'Tiger Eye', 'Citrine', 'Carnelian'],
  Virgo:       ['Sapphire', 'Peridot', 'Amazonite', 'Garnet'],
  Libra:       ['Opal', 'Lapis Lazuli', 'Rose Quartz', 'Tourmaline'],
  Scorpio:     ['Topaz', 'Amethyst', 'Black Tourmaline', 'Obsidian'],
  Sagittarius: ['Turquoise', 'Lapis Lazuli', 'Citrine', 'Sodalite'],
  Capricorn:   ['Garnet', 'Onyx', 'Smoky Quartz', 'Malachite'],
  Aquarius:    ['Amethyst', 'Aquamarine', 'Garnet', 'Fluorite'],
  Pisces:      ['Aquamarine', 'Amethyst', 'Moonstone', 'Labradorite'],
};

module.exports = ZODIAC_GEMS;


7.4 Engine Logic  —  controllers/recommendationController.js

const Gemstone       = require('../models/Gemstone');
const Recommendation = require('../models/Recommendation');
const ZODIAC_GEMS    = require('../data/recommendationMap');

exports.generate = async (req, res) => {
  try {
    const { zodiacSign, birthMonth, preference } = req.body;

    // Step 1: get candidate gemstone names from zodiac map
    const candidateNames = ZODIAC_GEMS[zodiacSign] || [];
    if (!candidateNames.length) {
      return res.status(400).json({ success: false, message: 'Invalid zodiac sign' });
    }

    // Step 2: DB query — zodiac + birth month + preference
    let results = await Gemstone.find({
      name:        { $in: candidateNames },
      birthMonths: birthMonth,
      category:    preference,
      inStock:     true
    }).limit(5);

    // Step 3: fallback to zodiac + preference only
    if (results.length < 3) {
      results = await Gemstone.find({
        name:     { $in: candidateNames },
        category: preference,
        inStock:  true
      }).limit(5);
    }

    // Step 4: final fallback — zodiac only
    if (results.length < 3) {
      results = await Gemstone.find({
        name:    { $in: candidateNames },
        inStock: true
      }).limit(5);
    }

    // Step 5: save to history
    const rec = await Recommendation.create({
      userId:     req.user._id,
      zodiacSign, birthMonth, preference,
      gemstones:  results.map(g => g._id)
    });

    res.json({ success: true, recommendationId: rec._id, gemstones: results });
  } catch (err) {
    res.status(500).json({ success: false, message: err.message });
  }
};

💡  This fallback chain guarantees the user always sees results. Start strict (all 3 criteria), then relax one at a time. Interviewers will appreciate this graceful degradation pattern.

async function seed() {
  await mongoose.connect(process.env.MONGODB_URI);
  await Gemstone.deleteMany({});
  await Gemstone.insertMany(gemstones);
  console.log('✅ 20 gemstones seeded');
  process.exit(0);
}

Backend  (.env)

PORT=5000
MONGODB_URI=mongodb+srv://<user>:<pass>@cluster0.mongodb.net/gemstone_db
JWT_SECRET=your_random_32_char_secret_here
CLIENT_URL=https://your-app.vercel.app

Frontend  (.env)

VITE_API_URL=https://your-backend.onrender.com/api


9.2 MongoDB Atlas Setup (5 minutes)
Go to mongodb.com/atlas → Create free M0 cluster
Create a database user (username + password)
Under Network Access → Add IP Address → Allow from Anywhere (0.0.0.0/0)
Click Connect → Drivers → Copy connection string into MONGODB_URI
Run seed: node data/seedGemstones.js

9.3 Backend Deployment — Render.com (Free)
Push backend code to GitHub repository
render.com → New Web Service → Connect GitHub repo
Build command:  npm install
Start command:  node server.js
Add all .env variables in the "Environment" panel
Deploy → copy the URL (e.g. https://gemstone-api.onrender.com)
⚠️  Render free tier spins down after 15 min of inactivity. First request after sleep takes ~30 seconds. This is fine for a placement demo.

9.4 Frontend Deployment — Vercel.com (Free)
Push frontend code to GitHub
vercel.com → New Project → Import GitHub repo
Framework Preset: Vite
Add environment variable: VITE_API_URL = your Render backend URL + /api
Deploy → Vercel gives you a live URL instantly

9.5 Admin Account Setup
After deployment, create an admin user directly in MongoDB Atlas:

// In MongoDB Atlas Data Explorer → gemstone_db → users collection
// Find your registered user and manually set:
{ "$set": { "role": "admin" } }

// Or run this one-time script locally:
// node -e "require('./config/db')(); const User = require('./models/User');
//   User.findOneAndUpdate({email:'admin@example.com'},{role:'admin'}).then(()=>process.exit())"
